Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ESTJ (Extraverted Sensing Thinking Judging) individual, you are likely organized, practical, and detail-oriented. You thrive in structured environments and prefer clear goals and plans. You make decisions based on facts and data, and you excel at managing tasks and projects efficiently. You value reliability, consistency, and tradition, often taking the lead in organizing activities and making sure everyone follows the rules. Your strong sense of duty and responsibility makes you reliable for those around you, but you might also come across as somewhat rigid or inflexible if change is not necessary or well-justified.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 4
results: [4]

You thrive in structured environments where you can apply your strong sense of duty and responsibility, often taking on leadership roles to ensure everything runs smoothly. Detail-oriented and decisive, you excel at problem-solving and making decisions based on facts and data. Your preference for routine and stability is evident in your meticulous planning and the way you structure your life. However, you might come across as somewhat inflexible or rigid, especially when it comes to change, as you value consistency and reliability above all else.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You are definitely not an artistic type of person
response: 7
results: [3, 7, 4, 6, 3, 4, 5, 7, 5, 3, 3, 6, 5, 2, 6, 3, 3, 5, 2, 5, 2, 7]

You excel at managing tasks and have a strong sense of duty, often taking on leadership roles. You prefer clear structures and routines, making you reliable and efficient in your interactions and decisions. Your decisiveness and attention to detail make you effective in problem-solving and goal achievement, but you might also come across as somewhat rigid or controlling if not balanced with more empathetic traits.

You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: When someone thinks highly of you, you wonder how long it will take them to feel disappointed in you
response: 7

You excel at prioritizing tasks and making decisions based on facts and logic, often taking charge of situations with a clear plan of action. Your strong sense of responsibility and commitment to efficiency make you a reliable team leader, yet you might sometimes come across as somewhat rigid or inflexible due to your preference for structured environments and systems. You value tradition and stability, which can influence your decision-making processes, but you also have a keen eye for detail and the ability to handle complex information effectively.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 4
results: [4]
